         <script>
          function showMenuNextLevel(element) {
         $('#submenubutton_' + element).parent().children('ul').toggle();
         if ($('#submenubutton_' + element).children('i').hasClass('fa-angle-double-right')) {
             $('#submenubutton_' + element).children('i').removeClass('fa-angle-double-right');
             $('#submenubutton_' + element).children('i').addClass('fa-angle-double-down');
         } else {
             $('#submenubutton_' + element).children('i').removeClass('fa-angle-double-down');
             $('#submenubutton_' + element).children('i').addClass('fa-angle-double-right');
         }
     }
         </script>

             <span class="lblRightBoxTitle" id="ctl00_ctl00_cphRightBoxes_ucRightBoxes_repRightBoxes_ctl02_lblRightBoxesContent">
              Heimat - und Wiesenfest
             </span>

           <div class="rightBoxContent">
            <script language="Javascript">
             var CountdownJahr6695 = 2019;
 var CountdownMonat6695 = 7;
 var CountdownTag6695 = 13;
 var CountdownStunde6695 = 19;
 var CountdownMinute6695 = 0;
 var CountdownSekunde6695 = 0;
 function CountdownAnzeigen6695()
  {
      var Jetzt = new Date();
      var Countdown6695 = new Date(CountdownJahr6695, CountdownMonat6695-1, CountdownTag6695, CountdownStunde6695, CountdownMinute6695, CountdownSekunde6695);
      var MillisekundenBisCountdown6695 = Countdown6695.getTime()-Jetzt.getTime();
      var Rest = Math.floor(MillisekundenBisCountdown6695/1000);
     var CountdownText6695 = '';
 	  if (Rest >= 31536000) 
      {
          var Jahre = Math.floor(Rest/31536000);
          Rest = Rest-Jahre*31536000;
         if(Jahre > 1 || Jahre == 0)
          {
              CountdownText6695 += Jahre + ' Jahre ';
          }
          else if(Jahre == 1)
          {
              CountdownText6695 += Jahre + ' Jahr ';
          }
      }
 		if (Rest >= 86400) 
      {
          var Tage = Math.floor(Rest/86400);
          Rest = Rest-Tage*86400;
         if(Tage > 1 || Tage == 0)
          {
              CountdownText6695 += Tage + ' Tage ';
          }
          else if(Tage == 1)
          {
              CountdownText6695 += Tage + ' Tag ';
          }
      }
 		if (Rest >= 3600) 
      {
          var Stunden = Math.floor(Rest/3600);
          Rest = Rest-Stunden*3600;
         if(Stunden > 1 || Stunden == 0)
          {
              CountdownText6695 += Stunden + ':';
          }
          else if(Stunden == 1)
          {
              CountdownText6695 += Stunden + ':';
          }
      }
 		if (Rest >= 60) 
      {
          var Minuten = Math.floor(Rest/60);
          Rest = Rest-Minuten*60;
         if(Minuten > 1 || Minuten == 0)
          {
              CountdownText6695 += Minuten + ':';
          }
          else if(Minuten == 1)
          {
              CountdownText6695 += Minuten + ':';
          }
      }
     if(Rest > 1 || Rest == 0)
      {
          CountdownText6695 += Rest + ' Stunden ';
      }
      else if(Rest==1)
      {
          CountdownText6695 += Rest + ' Stunden ';
      }
      document.getElementById('Countdown6695').innerHTML = CountdownText6695;
      window.setTimeout('CountdownAnzeigen6695()', 1000);
  }
            </script>
            <div style="position:relative;float:left;width:100%;height:100%;color:#000000;text-align:center;">
             <span class="Countdown" id="Countdown6695">
             </span>
            </div>
            <script language="Javascript">
             CountdownAnzeigen6695();
            </script>
